focus_tree = {
	id = british_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			original_tag  = ENG
		}
	}
	default = no 
 reset_on_civilwar = no

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 200 y = 4000 }

	###############################################################################################################################
	###############################################################################################################################
	###############################################################################################################################
	###############################################################################################################################
	##########DAWN OF A NEW CENTURY FOCUS##########################################################################################
	#################1900-1909#####################################################################################################

	###############################################################################################################################

#Focus for Negotiations With New Zealand
focus = {
	id = ENGDNC_negotiations_with_new_zealand
	icon = GFX_goal_tfv_strengthen_commonwealth_ties
	x = 56
	y = 8
	cost = 10
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	prerequisite = { focus = ENGDNC_negotiations_with_canada }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NZL
			}
			NZL = { country_event =  { id = dnc_eng.21 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = NZL }
			}
			every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = NZL
			}
			add_compliance = 5
			}
		}
	}
}
#Focus for His Majesty's Diplomatic Service

	id = ENGDNC_his_majestys_diplomatic_service

	x = 26
	y = 16
	cost = 1
	available_if_capitulated = yes

	allow_branch = {
		date < 1910.1.1
	}
		available = { 
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENGDNC_dieu_et_mon_droit }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENGDNC_british_democratic_tradition }
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
		}
	completion_reward = {
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

#Focus for Sign The Treaty of Vereeniging
focus = {
	id = ENGDNC_sign_the_treaty_of_vereeniging
	icon = GFX_focus_hol_the_foundations_of_defense
	x = 21
	y = 10
	cost = 10
	available = {
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = OFR
				country_exists = SRE
			}
			AND = {
				OFR = {
					is_subject_of = ENG

				}
				SRE = {
					is_subject_of = ENG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	prerequisite = { focus = ENGDNC_end_the_boer_war }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SRE
			}
			annex_country = { target = SRE }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = OFR
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = OFR
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SRE
					is_core_of = OFR
				}
			}
			add_compliance = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = ENG_second_boer_war
			}
			remove_ideas = ENG_second_boer_war
		}
		country_event =  { id = DNC_Expansion_country.19 }
		country_event =  { id = DNC_Expansion_country.33 }
	}
}

				}

					is_in_home_area = yes

						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}

		}
	}

focus = {
	id = ENG_DNC_support_middle_class
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_self_management
	x = -1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = ENG_DNC_free_market
	cost = 10
	prerequisite = {
		focus = ENG_DNC_free_market
	}
	completion_reward = {
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

						}

						building = dockyard
						size > 2
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = naval_effort_built
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					dockyard > 0

						building = dockyard

					}

			}

					}

						region = 1
						region = 2
						region = 3
					}
				}

					type = air_base
					level = 2

				}
				set_state_flag = air_rearmament_focus_2AirBase
			}

				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = air_base
						size > 1
					}
					OR = {
						region = 1
						region = 2
						region = 3
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = air_base
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = air_rearmament_focus_2AirBase
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = air_base
								size > 1
							}
							OR = {
								region = 1
								region = 2
								region = 3
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = air_base
							size > 1
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = air_base
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
					set_state_flag = air_rearmament_focus_2AirBase
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = air_base
							size > 1
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {

						level = 2

					}
					set_state_flag = air_rearmament_focus_2AirBase
				}
